class=\"sc-ikZCWJ eWTBpn  wui-text\"><span>The position</span></h3></div><div class=\"sc-brzPDJ iASsP sc-rSqkz hMKjv\"><div data-testid=\"job-section-description\" class=\"sc-brzPDJ kmwlVI\"><h4 class=\"sc-ikZCWJ cebuDO  wui-text\"><span>Job description</span></h4><div class=\"sc-brzPDJ kmwlVI\"><div data-is-text-too-long=\"true\" data-is-view-more=\"false\" class=\"sc-dBueTE jBdbxD\"><div class=\"sc-jHEWpz kgAAkN\"><p><b>About Mistral&nbsp;</b></p><p>At Mistral AI, we believe in the power of AI to simplify tasks, save time, and enhance learning and creativity. Our technology is designed to integrate seamlessly into daily working life.</p><p>We democratize AI through high-performance, optimized, open-source and cutting-edge models, products and solutions. Our comprehensive AI platform is designed to meet enterprise as well as personal needs. Our offerings include Le Chat, La Plateforme, Mistral Code and Mistral Compute - a suite that brings frontier intelligence to end-users.</p><p>We are a dynamic, collaborative team passionate about AI and its potential to transform society. Our diverse workforce thrives in competitive environments and is committed to driving innovation. Our teams are distributed between France, USA, UK, Germany and Singapore. We are creative, low-ego and team-spirited.</p><p>Join us to be part of a pioneering company shaping the future of AI. Together, we can make a meaningful impact. See more about our culture on https://mistral.ai/careers.</p><p><b>Role summary</b></p><p><span>We\u2019re seeking a strategic and execution-focused Product Manager to define and deliver the future of AI-generated audio and voice interfaces.&nbsp;We have recently released </span><a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://mistral.ai/fr/news/voxtral\">Voxtral</a><span>, our state\u2011of\u2011the\u2011art speech understanding models and this is only a first step in redefining AI-generated audio content. This is a ground-floor opportunity to turn research breakthroughs into scalable, transformative products. You\u2019ll own the strategy, roadmap, and execution for new interfaces, collaborating closely with research scientists, engineers, designers, and enterprise teams to bridge model innovation with real-world impact.</span></p><p><span>\ud83e\udde2 Reporting line: Product Director, Applications</span></p><p><span>\ud83d\udccd Location: New York, USA</span></p><p><b>What you will do</b></p><p><b>Define the Future</b></p><p><span>\u2022 Set the vision: Shape and evangelize a compelling product strategy for prosumer and enterprise-grade audio tools, ensuring alignment with company goals and market opportunities.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Spot the gaps: Lead market and UX research to uncover unmet needs, competitive whitespaces, and emerging trends in AI-driven audio and voice content.</span></p><p><b>Build &amp; Ship</b></p><p><span>\u2022 Own the lifecycle: Drive end-to-end product development, from ideation to launch and iteration\u2014balancing speed, quality, and user delight.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Champion the user: Partner with design and research to craft intuitive, high-impact experiences, using data and feedback to refine continuously.</span></p><p><b>Scale &amp; Execute</b></p><p><span>\u2022 Go-to-market: Collaborate with marketing and sales to launch products successfully, including pricing, positioning, and adoption strategies.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Align stakeholders: Rally engineering, design, and business teams around priorities, trade-offs, and timelines.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Prioritize ruthlessly: Maintain a dynamic roadmap that delivers quick wins while advancing long-term bets.</span></p><p><b>Required Qualifications</b></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Product Management</b><span>: 7+ years of relevant experience with a focus on building enterprise-grade AI products and features (B2B / B2B2C) </span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>AI/ML fluency</b><span>:</span><b>&nbsp;</b><span>Hands-on experience and/or deep technical understanding of ML-based systems \u2014 you understand technical trade-offs and can partner effectively with engineering teams.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Industry Expertise </b><span>: Knowledge of audio and voice agent architectures (STT/TTS/STS) </span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Problem-solving</b><span>: Experience in dynamic, competitive, and ambiguous environments</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>User obsession</b><span>: Relentless focus on solving real user problems, backed by data and qualitative insights.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Cross-functional influence</b><span>: Proven ability to align and inspire engineering, design, and go-to-market teams without direct authority.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Pragmatism: </b><span>Balance big-picture thinking with hands-on problem-solving \u2014 you\u2019re equally comfortable crafting a roadmap and diving into metrics.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Communication</b><span>: Crisp, persuasive storytelling for executives, teams, and users\u2014whether in docs, decks, or whiteboard sessions.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Adaptability</b><span>: Thrive in high-velocity, dynamic settings where priorities shift quickly.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Collaboration</b><span>: Low ego + high EQ \u2014 you build trust and drive decisions through clarity, not hierarchy.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Autonomy</b><span>: Self-directed with a bias for action, you own outcomes end-to-end.</span></p><p><span>Now, it would be ideal if you have:</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Industry experience with audio or voice products</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Builder\u2019s mindset: Founder or early-stage PM experience \u2014 you\u2019ve turned 0 \u2192 1 ideas into products users love.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Technical depth: Ability to prototype, hack, or dive into code when needed (even if not a core responsibility).</span></p><h3>What we offer</h3><li>\ud83d\udcb0 Competitive salary and equity.</li><li>\ud83d\ude91 Healthcare: Medical/Dental/Vision covered for you and your family.</li><li>\ud83d\udc74\ud83c\udffb Pension : 401K (6% matching)</li><li>\ud83c\udfdd\ufe0f PTO : 18 days&nbsp;</li><li>\ud83d\ude97 Transportation: Reimburse office parking charges, or $120/month for public transport</li><li>\ud83c\udfc0 Sport: $120/month reimbursement for gym membership</li><li>\ud83e\udd55 Meal stipend: $400 monthly allowance for meals (solution might evolve as we grow bigger)</li><li>\ud83c\udf0e Visa sponsorship&nbsp;</li><li>\ud83e\udd1d Coaching: we offer BetterUp coaching on a voluntary basis</li></div></div><div class=\"sc-izXThL gmvXFt  wui-text\"><a color=\"inherit\" data-testid=\"view-more-btn\" aria-expanded=\"false\" role=\"button\" eWTBpn  wui-text\"><span>The position</span></h3></div><div class=\"sc-brzPDJ iASsP sc-gitoGi csXUCJ\"><div data-testid=\"job-section-description\" class=\"sc-brzPDJ kmwlVI\"><h4 class=\"sc-ikZCWJ cebuDO  wui-text\"><span>Job description</span></h4><div class=\"sc-brzPDJ kmwlVI\"><div data-is-text-too-long=\"true\" data-is-view-more=\"false\" class=\"sc-fsUMhJ eSfIFL\"><div class=\"sc-jHEWpz kgAAkN\"><p><b>About Mistral&nbsp;</b></p><p>At Mistral AI, we believe in the power of AI to simplify tasks, save time, and enhance learning and creativity. Our technology is designed to integrate seamlessly into daily working life.</p><p>We democratize AI through high-performance, optimized, open-source and cutting-edge models, products and solutions. Our comprehensive AI platform is designed to meet enterprise as well as personal needs. Our offerings include Le Chat, La Plateforme, Mistral Code and Mistral Compute - a suite that brings frontier intelligence to end-users.</p><p>We are a dynamic, collaborative team passionate about AI and its potential to transform society. Our diverse workforce thrives in competitive environments and is committed to driving innovation. Our teams are distributed between France, USA, UK, Germany and Singapore. We are creative, low-ego and team-spirited.</p><p>Join us to be part of a pioneering company shaping the future of AI. Together, we can make a meaningful impact. See more about our culture on https://mistral.ai/careers.</p><p><b>Role summary</b></p><p><span>We\u2019re seeking a strategic and execution-focused Product Manager to define and deliver the future of AI-generated audio and voice interfaces.&nbsp;We have recently released </span><a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"https://mistral.ai/fr/news/voxtral\">Voxtral</a><span>, our state\u2011of\u2011the\u2011art speech understanding models and this is only a first step in redefining AI-generated audio content. This is a ground-floor opportunity to turn research breakthroughs into scalable, transformative products. You\u2019ll own the strategy, roadmap, and execution for new interfaces, collaborating closely with research scientists, engineers, designers, and enterprise teams to bridge model innovation with real-world impact.</span></p><p><span>\ud83e\udde2 Reporting line: Product Director, Applications</span></p><p><span>\ud83d\udccd Location: New York, USA</span></p><p><b>What you will do</b></p><p><b>Define the Future</b></p><p><span>\u2022 Set the vision: Shape and evangelize a compelling product strategy for prosumer and enterprise-grade audio tools, ensuring alignment with company goals and market opportunities.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Spot the gaps: Lead market and UX research to uncover unmet needs, competitive whitespaces, and emerging trends in AI-driven audio and voice content.</span></p><p><b>Build &amp; Ship</b></p><p><span>\u2022 Own the lifecycle: Drive end-to-end product development, from ideation to launch and iteration\u2014balancing speed, quality, and user delight.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Champion the user: Partner with design and research to craft intuitive, high-impact experiences, using data and feedback to refine continuously.</span></p><p><b>Scale &amp; Execute</b></p><p><span>\u2022 Go-to-market: Collaborate with marketing and sales to launch products successfully, including pricing, positioning, and adoption strategies.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Align stakeholders: Rally engineering, design, and business teams around priorities, trade-offs, and timelines.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Prioritize ruthlessly: Maintain a dynamic roadmap that delivers quick wins while advancing long-term bets.</span></p><p><b>Required Qualifications</b></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Product Management</b><span>: 7+ years of relevant experience with a focus on building enterprise-grade AI products and features (B2B / B2B2C) </span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>AI/ML fluency</b><span>:</span><b>&nbsp;</b><span>Hands-on experience and/or deep technical understanding of ML-based systems \u2014 you understand technical trade-offs and can partner effectively with engineering teams.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Industry Expertise </b><span>: Knowledge of audio and voice agent architectures (STT/TTS/STS) </span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Problem-solving</b><span>: Experience in dynamic, competitive, and ambiguous environments</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>User obsession</b><span>: Relentless focus on solving real user problems, backed by data and qualitative insights.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Cross-functional influence</b><span>: Proven ability to align and inspire engineering, design, and go-to-market teams without direct authority.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Pragmatism: </b><span>Balance big-picture thinking with hands-on problem-solving \u2014 you\u2019re equally comfortable crafting a roadmap and diving into metrics.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Communication</b><span>: Crisp, persuasive storytelling for executives, teams, and users\u2014whether in docs, decks, or whiteboard sessions.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Adaptability</b><span>: Thrive in high-velocity, dynamic settings where priorities shift quickly.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Collaboration</b><span>: Low ego + high EQ \u2014 you build trust and drive decisions through clarity, not hierarchy.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 </span><b>Autonomy</b><span>: Self-directed with a bias for action, you own outcomes end-to-end.</span></p><p><span>Now, it would be ideal if you have:</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Industry experience with audio or voice products</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Builder\u2019s mindset: Founder or early-stage PM experience \u2014 you\u2019ve turned 0 \u2192 1 ideas into products users love.</span></p><p><span>\u2022 Technical depth: Ability to prototype, hack, or dive into code when needed (even if not a core responsibility).</span></p><h3>What we offer</h3><li>\ud83d\udcb0 Competitive salary and equity.</li><li>\ud83d\ude91 Healthcare: Medical/Dental/Vision covered for you and your family.</li><li>\ud83d\udc74\ud83c\udffb Pension : 401K (6% matching)</li><li>\ud83c\udfdd\ufe0f PTO : 18 days&nbsp;</li><li>\ud83d\ude97 Transportation: Reimburse office parking charges, or $120/month for public transport</li><li>\ud83c\udfc0 Sport: $120/month reimbursement for gym membership</li><li>\ud83e\udd55 Meal stipend: $400 monthly allowance for meals (solution might evolve as we grow bigger)</li><li>\ud83c\udf0e Visa sponsorship&nbsp;</li><li>\ud83e\udd1d Coaching: we offer BetterUp coaching on a voluntary basis</li></div></div><div class=\"sc-izXThL gmvXFt  wui-text\"><a color=\"inherit\" data-testid=\"view-more-btn\" aria-expanded=\"false\" role=\"button\"
